<p>To celebrate Hari Merdeka &amp; Malaysia Day, <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="external text" href="https://www.facebook.com/entssea/">Team ENTs</a> are hosting <b>ENTs Hari Merdeka &amp; Hari Malaysia 2020</b>, an online Dota 2 Tournament with a total prize pool of 30,000 <abbr title="Malaysian ringgit">MYR</abbr>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Hari_Merdeka_Hari_Malaysia/2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants</b>
<ul><li>Eight team from open qualifiers</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Playoffs</b>
<ul><li>Double-elimination bracket</li>
<li>Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr>, all other matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Broadcast_Talent">Broadcast Talent</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Hari_Merdeka_Hari_Malaysia/2020&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Broadcast Talent">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Commentators:</b>
